<span class="pl-c">/\*_</span>
<span class="pl-c"> _ Get port from environment and store in Express.</span>
<span class="pl-c"> \*/</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">port</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">normalizePort</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">process</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">env</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">PORT</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s">'3000'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">set</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'port'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">port</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">/\*_</span>
<span class="pl-c"> _ Create HTTP server.</span>
<span class="pl-c"> \*/</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">server</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">http</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">createServer</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">app</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>github.com/i0natan/nodebestpractices</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q9: Rewrite the code sample without try/catch block ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q9-rewrite-the-code-sample-without-trycatch-block-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q9: Rewrite the code sample without try/catch block ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q9-rewrite-the-code-sample-without-trycatch-block-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">check</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">req</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">someOtherFunction</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">send</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"result"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">res</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">send</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">stack</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Rewrite the code sample without try/catch block.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">someOtherFunction</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">catch</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span><span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q10: How many threads does Node actually create? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q10-how-many-threads-does-node-actually-create-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q10: How many threads does Node actually create? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q10-how-many-threads-does-node-actually-create-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
<strong>4 extra threads</strong> are for use by V8. V8 uses these threads to perform various tasks, such as GC-related background tasks and optimizing compiler tasks.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>stackoverflow.com</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q11: Can Node.js work without V8? ☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q11-can-nodejs-work-without-v8-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q11: Can Node.js work without V8? ☆☆☆☆" href="#q11-can-nodejs-work-without-v8-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
No. The current node.js binary cannot work without V8. It would have no Javascript engine and thus no ability to run code which would obviously render it non-functional. Node.js was not designed to run with any other Javascript engine and, in fact, all the native code bindings that come with node.js (such as the fs module or the net module) all rely on the specific V8 interface between C++ and Javascript.</p>
<p dir="auto">There is an effort by Microsoft to allow the Chakra Javascript engine (that's the engine in Edge) to be used with node.js. Node.js can actually function to some extent without V8, through use of the node-chakracore project. There is ongoing work to reduce the tight coupling between V8 and Node, so that different JavaScript engines can be used in-place.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>stackoverflow.com</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q12: How the V8 engine works? ☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q12-how-the-v8-engine-works-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q12: How the V8 engine works? ☆☆☆☆" href="#q12-how-the-v8-engine-works-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
<strong>V8</strong> is a JavaScript engine built at the google development center, in Germany. It is open source and written in C++. It is used for both client side (Google Chrome) and server side (node.js) JavaScript applications.</p>
<p dir="auto">V8 was first designed to increase the performance of the JavaScript execution inside web browsers. In order to obtain speed, V8 translates JavaScript code into more efficient machine code instead of using an interpreter. It compiles JavaScript code into machine code at execution by implementing a <strong>JIT (Just-In-Time)</strong> compiler like a lot of modern JavaScript engines such as SpiderMonkey or Rhino (Mozilla) are doing. The main difference with V8 is that it doesn’t produce bytecode or any intermediate code.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>nodejs.org</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q13: What is the purpose of using hidden classes in V8? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q13-what-is-the-purpose-of-using-hidden-classes-in-v8-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q13: What is the purpose of using hidden classes in V8? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q13-what-is-the-purpose-of-using-hidden-classes-in-v8-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
JavaScript is a prototype-based language: there are no classes and objects are created by using a cloning process. JavaScript is also dynamically typed: types and type informations are not explicit and properties can be added to and deleted from objects on the fly.</p>
<p dir="auto">Accessing types and properties effectively makes a first big challenge for V8. Instead of using a dictionary-like data structure for storing object properties and doing a dynamic lookup to resolve the property location (like most JavaScript engines do), V8 creates** hidden classes**, at runtime, in order to have an internal representation of the type system and to improve the property access time.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>thibaultlaurens.github.io</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q14: How V8 compiles JavaScript code? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q14-how-v8-compiles-javascript-code-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q14: How V8 compiles JavaScript code? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q14-how-v8-compiles-javascript-code-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
V8 has two compilers:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">A <strong>“Full” Compiler</strong> that can generate good code for any JavaScript: good but not great JIT code. The goal of this compiler is to generate code quickly. To achieve its goal, it doesn’t do any type analysis and doesn’t know anything about types. Instead, it uses an Inline Caches or “IC” strategy to refine knowledge about types while the program runs. IC is very efficient and brings about 20 times speed improvment.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">An <strong>Optimizing Compiler</strong> that produces great code for most of the JavaScript language. It comes later and re-compiles hot functions. The optimizing compiler takes types from the Inline Cache and make decisions about how to optimize the code better. However, some language features are not supported yet like try/catch blocks for instance. (The workaround for try/catch blocks is to write the “non stable” code in a function and call the function in the try block)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">V8 also supports <strong>de-optimization</strong>: the optimizing compiler makes optimistic assumptions from the Inline Cache about the different types, de-optimization comes if these assumptions are invalid. For example, if a hidden class generated was not the one expected, V8 throws away the optimized code and comes back to the Full Compiler to get types again from the Inline Cache. This process is slow and should be avoided by trying to not change functions after they are optimized.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>thibaultlaurens.github.io</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q15: How does libuv work under the hood? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q15-how-does-libuv-work-under-the-hood-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q15: How does libuv work under the hood? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q15-how-does-libuv-work-under-the-hood-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
There is only one thread that executes JavaScript code and this is the thread where the event loop is running provided by <strong>libuv</strong>. The execution of callbacks (know that every userland code in a running Node.js application is a callback) is done by the event loop.</p>
<p dir="auto">Libuv by default creates a thread pool with four threads to offload asynchronous work to. Today’s operating systems already provide asynchronous interfaces for many I/O tasks (e.g. AIO on Linux).
Whenever possible, libuv will use those asynchronous interfaces, avoiding usage of the thread pool.</p>
<p dir="auto">The event loop as a process is a set of phases with specific tasks that are processed in a round-robin manner. Each phase has a FIFO queue of callbacks to execute. While each phase is special in its own way, generally, when the event loop enters a given phase, it will perform any operations specific to that phase, then execute callbacks in that phase's queue until the queue has been exhausted or the maximum number of callbacks has executed. When the queue has been exhausted or the callback limit is reached, the event loop will move to the next phase, and so on.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>timers</strong>: this phase executes callbacks scheduled by <code>setTimeout()</code> and <code>setInterval()</code>.</li>
<li><strong>pending callbacks</strong>: executes I/O callbacks deferred to the next loop iteration.</li>
<li><strong>idle, prepare</strong>: only used internally.</li>
<li><strong>poll</strong>: retrieve new I/O events; execute I/O related callbacks (almost all with the exception of close callbacks, the ones scheduled by timers, and <code>setImmediate()</code>); node will block here when appropriate.</li>
<li><strong>check</strong>: <code>setImmediate()</code> callbacks are invoked here.</li>
<li><strong>close callbacks</strong>: some close callbacks, e.g. <code>socket.on('close', ...)</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49400d3daf13b18c426eb7013fc8c2eace5340f5a0923c55ad7e71e838e8fa76/68747470733a2f2f63646e2d696d616765732d312e6d656469756d2e636f6d2f6d61782f3830302f312a524f786961767a374c655270496663675244453743412e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/49400d3daf13b18c426eb7013fc8c2eace5340f5a0923c55ad7e71e838e8fa76/68747470733a2f2f63646e2d696d616765732d312e6d656469756d2e636f6d2f6d61782f3830302f312a524f786961767a374c655270496663675244453743412e706e67" data-canonical-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/800/1*ROxiavz7LeRpIfcgRDE7CA.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>nodejs.org</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q16: How does the cluster module work? What’s the difference between it and a load balancer? ☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q16-how-does-the-cluster-module-work-whats-the-difference-between-it-and-a-load-balancer-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q16: How does the cluster module work? What’s the difference between it and a load balancer? ☆☆☆☆" href="#q16-how-does-the-cluster-module-work-whats-the-difference-between-it-and-a-load-balancer-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
The cluster module performs fork from your server (at that moment it is already an OS process), thus creating several slave processes. The cluster module supports two methods of distributing incoming connections.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">The first one (and the default one on all platforms except Windows), is the round-robin approach, where the master process listens on a port, accepts new connections and distributes them across the workers in a round-robin fashion, with some built-in smarts to avoid overloading a worker process.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The second approach is where the master process creates the listen socket and sends it to interested workers. The workers then accept incoming connections directly.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The difference between a cluster module and a load balancer is that instead of distributing load between processes, the balancer distributes requests.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>imasters.com</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q17: What is V8 Templates? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q17-what-is-v8-templates-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q17: What is V8 Templates? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q17-what-is-v8-templates-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
A template is a blueprint for JavaScript functions and objects. You can use a template to wrap C++ functions and data structures within JavaScript objects. V8 has two types of templates: Function Templates and Object Templates.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Function Template</strong> is the blueprint for a single function. You create a JavaScript instance of template by calling the template’s GetFunction method from within the context in which you wish to instantiate the JavaScript function. You can also associate a C++ callback with a function template which is called when the JavaScript function instance is invoked.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Object Template</strong> is used to configure objects created with function template as their constructor. You can associate two types of C++ callbacks with object templates: accessor callback and interceptor callback. Accessor callback is invoked when a specific object property is accessed by a script. Interceptor callback is invoked when any object property is accessed by a script. In a nutshell, you can wrap C++ objects\structures within JavaScript objects.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>blog.ghaiklor.com</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q18: Why do we need C++ Addons in Node.js? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q18-why-do-we-need-c-addons-in-nodejs-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q18: Why do we need C++ Addons in Node.js? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q18-why-do-we-need-c-addons-in-nodejs-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
<strong>Node.js Addons</strong> are dynamically-linked shared objects, written in C++, that can be loaded into Node.js using the require() function, and used just as if they were an ordinary Node.js module. They are used primarily to provide an interface between JavaScript running in Node.js and C/C++ libraries.</p>
<p dir="auto">There can be many reasons to write nodejs addons:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>You may want to access some native apis that is difficult using JS alone.</li>
<li>You may want to integrate a third party library written in C/C++ and use it directly in Node.js.</li>
<li>You may want to rewrite some of the modules in C++ for performance reasons.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">N-API (pronounced N as in the letter, followed by API) is an API for building native Addons.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>nodejs.org</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q19: Is it possible to use "Class" in Node.js? ☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q19-is-it-possible-to-use-class-in-nodejs-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q19: Is it possible to use &quot;Class&quot; in Node.js? ☆☆☆☆" href="#q19-is-it-possible-to-use-class-in-nodejs-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
With ES6, you are able to make "actual" classes just like this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Animal</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

    <span class="pl-en">print</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Name is :'</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto">You can export a class just like anything else:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-smi">module</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">exports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Animal</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto">Once imported into another module, then you can treat it as if it were defined in that file:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">Animal</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'./Animal'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Cat</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">Animal</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
...
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>stackoverflow.com</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q20: Why Node.js devs tend to lean towards the Module Requiring vs Dependency Injection? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q20-why-nodejs-devs-tend-to-lean-towards-the-module-requiring-vs-dependency-injection-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q20: Why Node.js devs tend to lean towards the Module Requiring vs Dependency Injection? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q20-why-nodejs-devs-tend-to-lean-towards-the-module-requiring-vs-dependency-injection-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
Dependency injection is somewhat the opposite of normal <em>module design</em>. In normal module design, a module uses <code>require()</code> to load in all the other modules that it needs with the goal of making it simple for the caller to use your module. The caller can just require() in your module and your module will load all the other things it needs.</p>
<p dir="auto">With dependency injection, rather than the module loading the things it needs, the caller is required to pass in things (usually objects) that the module needs. This can make certain types of testing easier and it can make mocking certain things for testing purposes easier.</p>
<p dir="auto">Modules and dependency injection are orthogonal: if you need dependency injection for testability or extensibility then use it. If not, importing modules is fine. The great thing about JS is that you can modify just about anything to achieve what you want. This comes in handy when it comes to testing.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>reddit.com</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q1: Explain the result of this code execution ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q1-explain-the-result-of-this-code-execution-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q1: Explain the result of this code execution ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q1-explain-the-result-of-this-code-execution-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q2: Explain the result of this code execution ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q2-explain-the-result-of-this-code-execution-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q2: Explain the result of this code execution ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q2-explain-the-result-of-this-code-execution-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Details:</strong>
Explain the result of this code execution</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">EventEmitter</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'events'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">crazy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">EventEmitter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1 fired!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event2'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event2'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event2 fired!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">setImmediate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event3'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event3'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event3 fired!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-en">setImmediate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
Shortly - the app will be run infinitely. Any function passed as the setImmediate() argument is a callback that's executed in the <em>next iteration</em> of the event loop. Without <code>setImmidiate</code> all callbacks are executed in a synchronous manner. With <code>setImmidiate</code> each call back executed as a part of next event loop iteration so no recursion/stuck occurs.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> <em>codementor.io</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 class="heading-element" dir="auto">Q3: What will happen when that code will be executed? ☆☆☆☆☆</h3><a id="user-content-q3-what-will-happen-when-that-code-will-be-executed-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Q3: What will happen when that code will be executed? ☆☆☆☆☆" href="#q3-what-will-happen-when-that-code-will-be-executed-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Details:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">What will happen when that code will be executed?</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-v">EventEmitter</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'events'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">crazy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">EventEmitter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1 fired!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">process</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event2'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event2'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event2 fired!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">process</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event3'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event3'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event3 fired!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">process</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">nextTick</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">crazy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">emit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'event1'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Answer:</strong>
It’ll get stuck! And if you wait long enough, about 30 seconds, it’ll eventually give you a “process out of memory” exception. Now, the problem is not stack overflow, it’s GC not being able to reclaim memory. Every handler has its own closure to access the crazy on the outer layer. This cost comes out of the heap. Though you might not be 100% why GC can't successfully get the memory back, you can probably guess that the program got stuck in some even loop phase because there’s always another <code>process.nextTick</code> callback to be processed. So essentially, the event loop is blocked completely.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> _codementor.io_Consider the code:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">resolve</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-en">setTimeout</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-en">resolve</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2000</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">What if we want to run a few different values through our function and add the result?</p>
<p dir="auto">Promise-based solution will be:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">addPromise</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Promise</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">resolve</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">20</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
                <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">30</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
                    <span class="pl-en">resolve</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-en">addPromise</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">sum</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">sum</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto">Async/Await solution will look like:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js" dir="auto"><pre><span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">addAsync</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">20</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">doubleAfter2Seconds</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">30</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-en">addAsync</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">then</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">sum</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">sum</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
